    var vars = {};
    var parts = window.location.href.replace(/[?&]+([^=&]+)=([^&]*)/gi, function(m,key,value) {
        vars[key] = value;
    });
    return vars;
}
function getUrlParam(param) {
    let value = "";
    //console.log(window.location.href);
    if(window.location.href.indexOf(param) > -1)
        value = getUrlVars()[param];
    return value;
}
function setCookie(name,value,days) {
    var expires = "";
    if (days) {
        var date = new Date();
        date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days*24*60*60*1000));
        expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();
    }
    document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "")  + expires + "; domain=.bitpanda.com; path=/";
}
function getCookie(name) {
    var nameEQ = name + "=";
    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
    for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
        var c = ca[i];
        while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
        if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
    }
    return null;
}
function eraseCookie(name) {   
    document.cookie = name + '=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT; domain=.bitpanda.com; path=/';
}
const s_id = getUrlParam('s_id');

        document.getElementById("js-filter-transactions").onkeyup = function (e) {
            $('#table-transaction-costs-body tr').hide();

Please note that high BTC and ETH withdrawal fees are a result of traffic in the respective networks. Low fees during periods when the traffic is high would result in delays that can be very long or in transactions not being executed at all. For this reason, we regularly adapt our withdrawal fees in order to adjust them to the current situation so that a transaction is confirmed as soon as possible. &nbsp; </p></div> </section></div> </section> <section class="uk-padding-small-bottom uk-padding-small-top uk-section"><div class="default uk-container"><section class="module-text uk-padding-small-bottom uk-padding-small-top uk-section uk-text-left uk-text-left@m"><div class="module-text__content"><h2>Bitpanda Technology Solutions: Applicable Limits for customers</h2> <ul><li>Minimum buy and sell asset amount is EUR 1.00 </li><li>The maximum daily number of trades per customers is 350 trades </li><li>The maximum single Bitpanda Stocks trade size is normally EUR 50,000, but in high risk situations and depending on market conditions we reserve the right to temporarily lower it to EUR 15,000 </li><li>Liquidation by Bitpanda and or balance transfers to an IBAN have a &nbsp;EUR 1.00 &nbsp;processing fee </li><li>In the instance that a Bitpanda client wishes to transfer their balance to their Bitpanda broker account, transaction limits will be subject to the applicable Bitpanda broker limits</li></ul></div> </section> </div> </section></section> <footer id="layout-footer"><footer class="footer footer_brand_3"><section class="footer__navbar footer__navbar--sm footer__navbar__gradient"><div class="uk-container"><div class="uk-flex-center uk-grid" uk-grid=""><div class="middle-menu-column uk-text-center uk-text-right@m uk-width-1-1 uk-width-auto@m uk-first-column"><ul></ul> </div> <div class="uk-second-column uk-text-center uk-text-right@m uk-width-1-1 uk-width-auto@m"><span>© Bitpanda GmbH</span> </div></div> </div> </section> </footer> </footer> <section class="bp-banner__container"><div class="bp-banner bp-banner--hidden bp-banner--closed" id="cookie-banner"><div class="bp-banner__content"><div class="bp-banner__content__text"><div><h4>The website uses cookies.</h4> We use cookies to optimize our services.
